jsaction="rcuQ6b:rcuQ6b" jscontroller="G7YeLc" class="details-section-contents show-more-container more"> <div jscontroller="NlxvWb">  <h1 aria-label="Description"></h1> <div itemprop="description" class="show-more-content text-body" style="max-height: 144px;"> <div jsname="C4s9Ed">This mobile application facilitates hassle free lodging of report with Delhi Police for article/document lost in Delhi<p>The complainant has to provide the following details :</p><p>+ Complainant's Name, Father's/Mother's Name, Address, Mobile No, Email ID,Place of Loss in Delhi, Date of Loss, Time of loss (optional)</p><p>+ Lost Article(s) with Description (upto 10)</p><p>+ Brief of complaint.</p><p>+ On lodging of Lost Report (after clicking register button), complainant will get LR no. and other details prompt of lodging the report with Delhi Police with option of View/Download and Save/Exit.</p><p>+ In case saved, complainant can retrieve it in future by clicking the retrieve button.</p><p>+ On prompt complainant will also get link to generate and view the report.</p><p>Any agency or an individual has an option to verify the authenticity of the report, by entering the LR no by visiting the website of Delhi Police i.e. http://delhipolice.nic.in</p><p>To Access this application, users should have proper data / WiFi connection to</p><p></p><p></p><p></p><p></p><p></p><p></p><p></p><p></p></div>  <div class="show-more-end"></div> </div> </div> <div>  <button jsaction="KoToPc" class="play-button show-more small">Read
